+I have enough information to deliver the verdict.
+
+---
+
+VERDICT: **FAIL**
+
+FINDINGS:
+
+- **[High]** `OnboardingView.tsx` calls `getTemporalShowLabel()` at module-level (line 21, inside the `steps` array literal). This evaluates once at import time and bakes in whatever time-of-day the app launched. No unit test verifies that re-rendering at a different hour produces the correct label. The temporal property tests pass a `Date` argument to `getTemporalShowLabel(date)` but never test the `default = new Date()` path or the fact that the component freezes it at import time. (`src/renderer/views/OnboardingView.tsx:21`)
+
+- **[High]** Multiple E2E tests silently pass on failure via `.catch(() => false)` + `if (isVisible)` guard patterns — assertions inside the `if` block never fire if the element is absent. Examples: `visual-validation.test.ts:57-63` (beat ignite), `visual-validation.test.ts:102-104` (spotlight-golden), `visual-validation.test.ts:132-143` (#1 Claude), `visual-validation.test.ts:166-170` (#2 celebration), `visual-validation.test.ts:181-183` (#7 onair-glow). These tests can never fail — a genuine regression would be silently swallowed.
+
+- **[High]** `writers-room.test.ts:46-61` — test `'can submit plan and see lineup preview'` has no self-contained fixture setup and depends on the prior test's state (prior energy selection + plan fill). If run in isolation or if the prior test fails, the "Build my lineup" button won't exist, and both branches silently pass via `.catch(() => false)`. No assertion fires on the expected happy path. (`e2e/writers-room.test.ts:46`)
+
+- **[High]** `writers-room.test.ts:63-70` — test `'can go live'` is entirely conditional: if the go-live button isn't visible (which requires prior tests to have run in sequence), no assertion executes at all. This is a no-op test that always passes. (`e2e/writers-room.test.ts:63`)
+
+- **[Medium]** No E2E test verifies the OnboardingView temporal copy change. The onboarding test navigates through steps and checks titles ("The Writer's Room") but never asserts the step 2 body text uses the temporal label instead of hardcoded "tonight." This is the only source file changed outside of test/infrastructure files and has zero corresponding test coverage for the change. (`e2e/onboarding.test.ts`)
+
+- **[Medium]** `onboarding.test.ts:158-177` — `'Help button re-triggers onboarding'` wraps all assertions inside `if (await helpBtn.isVisible(...))`, meaning if the help button doesn't render, the entire test silently passes with zero assertions. (`e2e/onboarding.test.ts:166`)
+
+- **[Medium]** Temporal E2E tests (`temporal.test.ts`) use `seedFixture` which sets state via localStorage but don't mock the clock. The `getTemporalShowLabel()` call uses `new Date()` at runtime, so "today's lineup" vs "your next" vs "tomorrow's lineup" depends on when CI runs. A test passing at 9 AM will fail at 2 PM if the assertion expects a specific label. The test only asserts the label is NOT "tonight" and IS one of three options — but this makes it impossible to write a deterministic temporal assertion. (`e2e/temporal.test.ts:15-18`)
+
+- **[Low]** 2 E2E tests are currently failing (per `test-results/.last-run.json`) and static analysis reports a syntax error in `OnboardingView.tsx`. These should be resolved before merging. (`.loki/quality/static-analysis.json`, `test-results/.last-run.json`)
+
+- **[Low]** No test covers the `onSkip` prop fallback to `onComplete` when `onSkip` is undefined (`OnboardingView.tsx:73`: `onClick={onSkip || onComplete}`). The skip test exists but doesn't verify what happens when `onSkip` is not provided vs. when it is. (`src/renderer/views/OnboardingView.tsx:73`)
